192→\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n   193→\t\t\tdelete(victimBatch, wa)\n   194→\t\t\tbreak\n   195→\t\t}\n   196→\n   197→\t\t// victim being processed so not accessible; retry\n   198→\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   199→\t\ttime.Sleep(time.Millisecond)\n   200→\t}\n   201→\n   202→\twa.ch = nil\n   203→\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   204→}\n   205→\n   206→func (s *watchableStore) Restore(b backend.Backend) error {\n   207→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   208→\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n   209→\terr := s.store.Restore(b)\n   210→\tif err != nil {\n   211→\t\treturn err\n   212→\t}\n   213→\n   214→\tfor wa := range s.synced.watchers {\n   215→\t\twa.restore = true\n   216→\t\ts.unsynced.add(wa)\n   217→\t}\n   218→\ts.synced = newWatcherGroup()\n   219→\treturn nil\n   220→}\n   221→\n   222→// syncWatchersLoop syncs the watcher in the unsynced map every 100ms.\n   223→func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchersLoop() {\n   224→\tdefer s.wg.Done()\n   225→\n   226→\tdelayTicker := time.NewTicker(watchResyncPeriod)\n   227→\tdefer delayTicker.Stop()\n   228→\tvar evs []mvccpb.Event\n   229→\n   230→\tfor {\n   231→\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n   232→\t\tst := time.Now()\n   233→\t\tlastUnsyncedWatchers := s.unsynced.size()\n   234→\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n   235→\n   236→\t\tunsyncedWatchers := 0\n   237→\t\tif lastUnsyncedWatchers > 0 {\n   238→\t\t\tunsyncedWatchers, evs = s.syncWatchers(evs)\n   239→\t\t}\n   240→\t\tsyncDuration := time.Since(st)\n   241→\n   242→\t\tdelayTicker.Reset(watchResyncPeriod)\n   243→\t\t// more work pending?\n   244→\t\tif unsyncedWatchers != 0 && lastUnsyncedWatchers > unsyncedWatchers {\n   245→\t\t\t// be fair to other store operations by yielding time taken\n   246→\t\t\tdelayTicker.Reset(syncDuration)\n   247→\t\t}\n   248→\n   249→\t\tselect {\n   250→\t\tcase <-delayTicker.C:\n   251→\t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n   252→\t\t\treturn\n   253→\t\t}\n   254→\t}\n   255→}\n   256→\n   257→// syncVictimsLoop tries to write precomputed watcher responses to\n   258→// watchers that had a blocked watcher channel\n   259→func (s *watchableStore) syncVictimsLoop() {\n   260→\tdefer s.wg.Done()\n   261→\n   262→\tfor {\n   263→\t\tfor s.moveVictims() != 0 {\n   264→\t\t\t// try to update all victim watchers\n   265→\t\t}\n   266→\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n   267→\t\tisEmpty := len(s.victims) == 0\n   268→\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n   269→\n   270→\t\tvar tickc <-chan time.Time\n   271→\t\tif !isEmpty {\n   272→\t\t\ttickc = time.After(10 * time.Millisecond)\n   273→\t\t}\n   274→\n   275→\t\tselect {\n   276→\t\tcase <-tickc:\n   277→\t\tcase <-s.victimc:\n   278→\t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n   279→\t\t\treturn\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\t}\n   282→}\n   283→\n   284→// moveVictims tries to update watches with already pending event data\n   285→func (s *watchableStore) moveVictims() (moved int) {\n   286→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   287→\tvictims := s.victims\n   288→\ts.victims = nil\n   289→\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   290→\n   291→\tvar newVictim watcherBatch\n   292→\tfor _, wb := range victims {\n   293→\t\t// try to send responses again\n   294→\t\tfor w, eb := range wb {\n   295→\t\t\t// watcher has observed the store up to, but not including, w.minRev\n   296→\t\t\trev := w.minRev - 1\n   297→\t\t\tif !w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: rev}) {\n   298→\t\t\t\tif newVictim == nil {\n   299→\t\t\t\t\tnewVictim = make(watcherBatch)\n   300→\t\t\t\t}\n   301→\t\t\t\tnewVictim[w] = eb\n   302→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   303→\t\t\t}\n   304→\t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n   305→\t\t\tmoved++\n   306→\t\t}\n   307→\n   308→\t\t// assign completed victim watchers to unsync/sync\n   309→\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n   310→\t\ts.store.revMu.RLock()\n   311→\t\tcurRev := s.store.currentRev\n   312→\t\tfor w, eb := range wb {\n   313→\t\t\tif newVictim != nil && newVictim[w] != nil {\n   314→\t\t\t\t// couldn't send watch response; stays victim\n   315→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   316→\t\t\t}\n   317→\t\t\tw.victim = false\n   318→\t\t\tif eb.moreRev != 0 {\n   319→\t\t\t\tw.minRev = eb.moreRev\n   320→\t\t\t}\n   321→\t\t\tif w.minRev <= curRev {\n   322→\t\t\t\ts.unsynced.add(w)\n   323→\t\t\t} else {\n   324→\t\t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\n   325→\t\t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n   326→\t\t\t}\n   327→\t\t}\n   328→\t\ts.store.revMu.RUnlock()\n   329→\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   330→\t}\n   331→\n   332→\tif len(newVictim) > 0 {\n   333→\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n   334→\t\ts.victims = append(s.victims, newVictim)\n   335→\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   336→\t}\n   337→\n   338→\treturn moved\n   339→}\n   340→\n   341→// syncWatchers syncs unsynced watchers by:\n   342→//  1. choose a set of watchers from the unsynced watcher group\n   343→//  2. iterate over the set to get the minimum revision and remove compacted watchers\n   344→//  3. use minimum revision to get all key-value pairs and send those events to watchers\n   345→//  4. remove synced watchers in set from unsynced group and move to synced group\n   346→func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchers(evs []mvccpb.Event) (int, []mvccpb.Event) {\n   347→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   348→\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n   349→\n   350→\tif s.unsynced.size() == 0 {\n   351→\t\treturn 0, []mvccpb.Event{}\n   352→\t}\n   353→\n   354→\ts.store.revMu.RLock()\n   355→\tdefer s.store.revMu.RUnlock()\n   356→\n   357→\t// in order to find key-value pairs from unsynced watchers, we need to\n   358→\t// find min revision index, and these revisions can be used to\n   359→\t// query the backend store of key-value pairs\n   360→\tcurRev := s.store.currentRev\n   361→\tcompactionRev := s.store.compactMainRev\n   362→\n   363→\twg, minRev := s.unsynced.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactionRev)\n   364→\tevs = rangeEventsWithReuse(s.store.lg, s.store.b, evs, minRev, curRev+1)\n   365→\n   366→\tvictims := make(watcherBatch)\n   367→\twb := newWatcherBatch(wg, evs)\n   368→\tfor w := range wg.watchers {\n   369→\t\tif w.minRev < compactionRev {\n   370→\t\t\t// Skip the watcher that failed to send compacted watch response due to w.ch is full.\n   371→\t\t\t// Next retry of syncWatchers would try to resend the compacted watch response to w.ch\n   372→\t\t\tcontinue\n   373→\t\t}\n   374→\t\tw.minRev = max(curRev+1, w.minRev)\n   375→\n   376→\t\teb, ok := wb[w]\n   377→\t\tif !ok {\n   378→\t\t\t// bring un-notified watcher to synced\n   379→\t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n   380→\t\t\ts.unsynced.delete(w)\n   381→\t\t\tcontinue\n   382→\t\t}\n   383→\n   384→\t\tif eb.moreRev != 0 {\n   385→\t\t\tw.minRev = eb.moreRev\n   386→\t\t}\n   387→\n   388→\t\tif w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: curRev}) {\n   389→\t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n   390→\t\t} else {\n   391→\t\t\tw.victim = true\n   392→\t\t}\n   393→\n   394→\t\tif w.victim {\n   395→\t\t\tvictims[w] = eb\n   396→\t\t} else {\n   397→\t\t\tif eb.moreRev != 0 {\n   398→\t\t\t\t// stay unsynced; more to read\n   399→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   400→\t\t\t}\n   401→\t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n   402→\t\t}\n   403→\t\ts.unsynced.delete(w)\n   404→\t}\n   405→\ts.addVictim(victims)\n   406→\n   407→\tvsz := 0\n   408→\tfor _, v := range s.victims {\n   409→\t\tvsz += len(v)\n   410→\t}\n   411→\tslowWatcherGauge.Set(float64(s.unsynced.size() + vsz))\n   412→\n   413→\treturn s.unsynced.size(), evs\n   414→}\n   415→\n   416→// rangeEventsWithReuse returns events in range [minRev, maxRev), while reusing already provided events.\n   417→func rangeEventsWithReuse(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, evs []mvccpb.Event, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n   418→\tif len(evs) == 0 {\n   419→\t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n   420→\t}\n   421→\t// append from left\n   422→\tif evs[0].Kv.ModRevision > minRev {\n   423→\t\tevs = append(rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, evs[0].Kv.ModRevision), evs...)\n   424→\t}\n   425→\t// cut from left\n   426→\tprefixIndex := 0\n   427→\tfor prefixIndex < len(evs) && evs[prefixIndex].Kv.ModRevision < minRev {\n   428→\t\tprefixIndex++\n   429→\t}\n   430→\tevs = evs[prefixIndex:]\n   431→\n   432→\tif len(evs) == 0 {\n   433→\t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n   434→\t}\n   435→\t// append from right\n   436→\tif evs[len(evs)-1].Kv.ModRevision+1 < maxRev {\n   437→\t\tevs = append(evs, rangeEvents(lg, b, evs[len(evs)-1].Kv.ModRevision+1, maxRev)...)\n   438→\t}\n   439→\t// cut from right\n   440→\tsuffixIndex := len(evs) - 1\n   441→\tfor suffixIndex >= 0 && evs[suffixIndex].Kv.ModRevision >= maxRev {\n   442→\t\tsuffixIndex--\n   443→\t}\n   444→\tevs = evs[:suffixIndex+1]\n   445→\treturn evs\n   446→}\n   447→\n   448→// rangeEvents returns events in range [minRev, maxRev).\n   449→func rangeEvents(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n   450→\tif minRev < 0 {\n   451→\t\tlg.Warn(\"Unexpected negative revision range start\", zap.Int64(\"minRev\", minRev))\n   452→\t\tminRev = 0\n   453→\t}\n   454→\tminBytes, maxBytes := NewRevBytes(), NewRevBytes()\n   455→\tminBytes = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: minRev}, minBytes)\n   456→\tmaxBytes = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: maxRev}, maxBytes)\n   457→\n   458→\t// UnsafeRange returns keys and values. And in boltdb, keys are revisions.\n   459→\t// values are actual key-value pairs in backend.\n   460→\ttx := b.ReadTx()\n   461→\ttx.RLock()\n   462→\trevs, vs := tx.UnsafeRange(schema.Key, minBytes, maxBytes, 0)\n   463→\tevs := kvsToEvents(lg, revs, vs)\n   464→\t// Must unlock after kvsToEvents, because vs (come from boltdb memory) is not deep copy.\n   465→\t// We can only unlock after Unmarshal, which will do deep copy.\n   466→\t// Otherwise we will trigger SIGSEGV during boltdb re-mmap.\n   467→\ttx.RUnlock()\n   468→\treturn evs\n   469→}\n   470→\n   471→// kvsToEvents gets all events for the watchers from all key-value pairs\n   472→func kvsToEvents(lg *zap.Logger, revs, vals [][]byte) (evs []mvccpb.Event) {\n   473→\tfor i, v := range vals {\n   474→\t\tvar kv mvccpb.KeyValue\n   475→\t\tif err := kv.Unmarshal(v); err != nil {\n   476→\t\t\tlg.Panic(\"failed to unmarshal mvccpb.KeyValue\", zap.Error(err))\n   477→\t\t}\n   478→\n   479→\t\tty := mvccpb.Event_PUT\n   480→\t\tif isTombstone(revs[i]) {\n   481→\t\t\tty = mvccpb.Event_DELETE\n   482→\t\t\t// patch in mod revision so watchers won't skip\n   483→\t\t\tkv.ModRevision = BytesToRev(revs[i]).Main\n   484→\t\t}\n   485→\t\tevs = append(evs, mvccpb.Event{Kv: &kv, Type: ty})\n   486→\t}\n   487→\treturn evs\n   488→}\n   489→\n   490→// notify notifies the fact that given event at the given rev just happened to\n   491→// watchers that watch on the key of the event.\n   492→func (s *watchableStore) notify(rev int64, evs []mvccpb.Event) {\n   493→\tvictim := make(watcherBatch)\n   494→\tfor w, eb := range newWatcherBatch(&s.synced, evs) {\n   495→\t\tif eb.revs != 1 {\n   496→\t\t\ts.store.lg.Panic(\n   497→\t\t\t\t\"unexpected multiple revisions in watch notification\",\n   498→\t\t\t\tzap.Int(\"number-of-revisions\", eb.revs),\n   499→\t\t\t)\n   500→\t\t}\n   501→\t\tif w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: rev}) {\n   502→\t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n   503→\t\t} else {\n   504→\t\t\t// move slow watcher to victims\n   505→\t\t\tw.victim = true\n   506→\t\t\tvictim[w] = eb\n   507→\t\t\ts.synced.delete(w)\n   508→\t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Inc()\n   509→\t\t}\n   510→\t\t// always update minRev\n   511→\t\t// in case 'send' returns true and watcher stays synced, this is needed for Restore when all watchers become unsynced\n   512→\t\t// in case 'send' returns false, this is needed for syncWatchers\n   513→\t\tw.minRev = rev + 1\n   514→\t}\n   515→\ts.addVictim(victim)\n   516→}\n   517→\n   518→func (s *watchableStore) addVictim(victim watcherBatch) {\n   519→\tif len(victim) == 0 {\n   520→\t\treturn\n   521→\t}\n   522→\ts.victims = append(s.victims, victim)\n   523→\tselect {\n   524→\tcase s.victimc <- struct{}{}:\n   525→\tdefault:\n   526→\t}\n   527→}\n   528→\n   529→func (s *watchableStore) rev() int64 { return s.store.Rev() }\n   530→\n   531→func (s *watchableStore) progress(w *watcher) {\n   532→\ts.progressIfSync(map[WatchID]*watcher{w.id: w}, w.id)\n   533→}\n   534→\n   535→func (s *watchableStore) progressAll(watchers map[WatchID]*watcher) bool {\n   536→\treturn s.progressIfSync(watchers, clientv3.InvalidWatchID)\n   537→}\n   538→\n   539→func (s *watchableStore) progressIfSync(watchers map[WatchID]*watcher, responseWatchID WatchID) bool {\n   540→\ts.mu.RLock()\n   541→\tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()\n   542→\n   543→\trev := s.rev()\n   544→\t// Any watcher unsynced?\n   545→\tfor _, w := range watchers {\n   546→\t\tif _, ok := s.synced.watchers[w]; !ok {\n   547→\t\t\treturn false\n   548→\t\t}\n   549→\t\tif rev < w.startRev {\n   550→\t\t\treturn false\n   551→\t\t}\n   552→\t}\n   553→\n   554→\t// If all watchers are synchronised, send out progress\n   555→\t// notification on first watcher. Note that all watchers\n   556→\t// should have the same underlying stream, and the progress\n   557→\t// notification will be broadcasted client-side if required\n   558→\t// (see dispatchEvent in client/v3/watch.go)\n   559→\tfor _, w := range watchers {\n   560→\t\tw.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: responseWatchID, Revision: rev})\n   561→\t\treturn true\n   562→\t}\n   563→\treturn true\n   564→}\n   565→\n   566→type watcher struct {\n   567→\t// the watcher key\n   568→\tkey []byte\n   569→\t// end indicates the end of the range to watch.\n   570→\t// If end is set, the watcher is on a range.\n   571→\tend []byte\n   572→\n   573→\t// victim is set when ch is blocked and undergoing victim processing\n   574→\tvictim bool\n   575→\n   576→\t// compacted is set when the watcher is removed because of compaction\n   577→\tcompacted bool\n   578→\n   579→\t// restore is true when the watcher is being restored from leader snapshot\n   580→\t// which means that this watcher has just been moved from \"synced\" to \"unsynced\"\n   581→\t// watcher group, possibly with a future revision when it was first added\n   582→\t// to the synced watcher\n   583→\t// \"unsynced\" watcher revision must always be <= current revision,\n   584→\t// except when the watcher were to be moved from \"synced\" watcher group\n   585→\trestore bool\n   586→\n   587→\tstartRev int64\n   588→\t// minRev is the minimum revision update the watcher will accept\n   589→\tminRev int64\n   590→\tid     WatchID\n   591→\n   592→\tfcs []FilterFunc\n   593→\t// a chan to send out the watch response.\n   594→\t// The chan might be shared with other watchers.\n   595→\tch chan<- WatchResponse\n   596→}\n   597→\n   598→func (w *watcher) send(wr WatchResponse) bool {\n   599→\tprogressEvent := len(wr.Events) == 0\n   600→\n   601→\tif len(w.fcs) != 0 {\n   602→\t\tne := make([]mvccpb.Event, 0, len(wr.Events))\n   603→\t\tfor i := range wr.Events {\n   604→\t\t\tfiltered := false\n   605→\t\t\tfor _, filter := range w.fcs {\n   606→\t\t\t\tif filter(wr.Events[i]) {\n   607→\t\t\t\t\tfiltered = true\n   608→\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   609→\t\t\t\t}\n   610→\t\t\t}\n   611→\t\t\tif !filtered {\n   612→\t\t\t\tne = append(ne, wr.Events[i])\n   613→\t\t\t}\n   614→\t\t}\n   615→\t\twr.Events = ne\n   616→\t}\n   617→\n   618→\tverify.Verify(\"Event.ModRevision is less than the w.startRev for watchID\", func() (bool, map[string]any) {\n   619→\t\tif w.startRev > 0 {\n   620→\t\t\tfor _, ev := range wr.Events {\n   621→\t\t\t\tif ev.Kv.ModRevision < w.startRev {\n   622→\t\t\t\t\treturn false, map[string]any{\n   623→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"Event.ModRevision\": ev.Kv.ModRevision,\n   624→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"w.startRev\":        w.startRev,\n   625→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"watchID\":           w.id,\n   626→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   627→\t\t\t\t}\n   628→\t\t\t}\n   629→\t\t}\n   630→\t\treturn true, nil\n   631→\t})\n   632→\n   633→\t// if all events are filtered out, we should send nothing.\n   634→\tif !progressEvent && len(wr.Events) == 0 {\n   635→\t\treturn true\n   636→\t}\n   637→\tselect {\n   638→\tcase w.ch <- wr:\n   639→\t\treturn true\n   640→\tdefault:\n   641→\t\treturn false\n   642→\t}\n   643→}\n   644→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. non-const so modifiable by tests\nvar (\n\t// chanBufLen is the length of the buffered chan\n\t// for sending out watched events.\n\t// See https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/issues/11906 for more detail.\n\tchanBufLen = 128\n\n\t// maxWatchersPerSync is the number of watchers to sync in a single batch\n\tmaxWatchersPerSync = 512\n\n\t// maxResyncPeriod is the period of executing resync.\n\twatchResyncPeriod = 100 * time.Millisecond\n)\n\nfunc ChanBufLen() int { return chanBufLen }\n\ntype watchable interface {\n\twatch(key, end []byte, startRev int64, id WatchID, ch chan<- WatchResponse, fcs ...FilterFunc) (*watcher, cancelFunc)\n\tprogress(w *watcher)\n\tprogressAll(watchers map[WatchID]*watcher) bool\n\trev() int64\n}\n\ntype watchableStore struct {\n\t*store\n\n\t// mu protects watcher groups and batches. It should never be locked\n\t// before locking store.mu to avoid deadlock.\n\tmu sync.RWMutex\n\n\t// victims are watcher batches that were blocked on the watch channel\n\tvictims []watcherBatch\n\tvictimc chan struct{}\n\n\t// contains all unsynced watchers that needs to sync with events that have happened\n\tunsynced watcherGroup\n\n\t// contains all synced watchers that are in sync with the progress of the store.\n\t// The key of the map is the key that the watcher watches on.\n\tsynced watcherGroup\n\n\tstopc chan struct{}\n\twg    sync.WaitGroup\n}\n\nvar _ WatchableKV = (*watchableStore)(nil)\n\n// cancelFunc updates unsynced and synced maps when running\n// cancel operations.\ntype cancelFunc func()\n\nfunc New(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, le lease.Lessor, cfg StoreConfig) WatchableKV {\n\ts := newWatchableStore(lg, b, le, cfg)\n\ts.wg.Add(2)\n\tgo s.syncWatchersLoop()\n\tgo s.syncVictimsLoop()\n\treturn s\n}\n\nfunc newWatchableStore(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, le lease.Lessor, cfg StoreConfig) *watchableStore {\n\tif lg == nil {\n\t\tlg = zap.NewNop()\n\t}\n\ts := &watchableStore{\n\t\tstore:    NewStore(lg, b, le, cfg),\n\t\tvictimc:  make(chan struct{}, 1),\n\t\tunsynced: newWatcherGroup(),\n\t\tsynced:   newWatcherGroup(),\n\t\tstopc:    make(chan struct{}),\n\t}\n\ts.store.ReadView = &readView{s}\n\ts.store.WriteView = &writeView{s}\n\tif s.le != nil {\n\t\t// use this store as the deleter so revokes trigger watch events\n\t\ts.le.SetRangeDeleter(func() lease.TxnDelete { return s.Write(traceutil.TODO()) })\n\t}\n\treturn s\n}\n\nfunc (s *watchableStore) Close() error {\n\tclose(s.stopc)\n\ts.wg.Wait()\n\treturn s.store.Close()\n}\n\nfunc (s *watchableStore) NewWatchStream() WatchStream {\n\twatchStreamGauge.Inc()\n\treturn &watchStream{\n\t\twatchable: s,\n\t\tch:        make(chan WatchResponse, chanBufLen),\n\t\tcancels:   make(map[WatchID]cancelFunc),\n\t\twatchers:  make(map[WatchID]*watcher),\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (s *watchableStore) watch(key, end []byte, startRev int64, id WatchID, ch chan<- WatchResponse, fcs ...FilterFunc) (*watcher, cancelFunc) {\n\twa := &watcher{\n\t\tkey:      key,\n\t\tend:      end,\n\t\tstartRev: startRev,\n\t\tminRev:   startRev,\n\t\tid:       id,\n\t\tch:       ch,\n\t\tfcs:      fcs,\n\t}\n\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\ts.revMu.RLock()\n\tsynced := startRev > s.store.currentRev || startRev == 0\n\tif synced {\n\t\twa.minRev = s.store.currentRev + 1\n\t\tif startRev > wa.minRev {\n\t\t\twa.minRev = startRev\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.synced.add(wa)\n\t} else {\n\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Inc()\n\t\ts.unsynced.add(wa)\n\t}\n\ts.revMu.RUnlock()\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\twatcherGauge.Inc()\n\n\treturn wa, func() { s.cancelWatcher(wa) }\n}\n\n// cancelWatcher removes references of the watcher from the watchableStore\nfunc (s *watchableStore) cancelWatcher(wa *watcher) {\n\tfor {\n\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n\t\tif s.unsynced.delete(wa) {\n\t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t} else if s.synced.delete(wa) {\n\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t} else if wa.ch == nil {\n\t\t\t// already canceled (e.g., cancel/close race)\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t} else if wa.compacted {\n\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif !wa.victim {\n\t\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\tpanic(\"watcher not victim but not in watch groups\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar victimBatch watcherBatch\n\t\tfor _, wb := range s.victims {\n\t\t\tif wb[wa] != nil {\n\t\t\t\tvictimBatch = wb\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif victimBatch != nil {\n\t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\tdelete(victimBatch, wa)\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// victim being processed so not accessible; retry\n\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\t\ttime.Sleep(time.Millisecond)\n\t}\n\n\twa.ch = nil\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n}\n\nfunc (s *watchableStore) Restore(b backend.Backend) error {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\terr := s.store.Restore(b)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tfor wa := range s.synced.watchers {\n\t\twa.restore = syncWatchersLoop() {\n\tdefer s.wg.Done()\n\n\tdelayTicker := time.NewTicker(watchResyncPeriod)\n\tdefer delayTicker.Stop()\n\tvar evs []mvccpb.Event\n\n\tfor {\n\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n\t\tst := time.Now()\n\t\tlastUnsyncedWatchers := s.unsynced.size()\n\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t\tunsyncedWatchers := 0\n\t\tif lastUnsyncedWatchers > 0 {\n\t\t\tunsyncedWatchers, evs = unsyncedWatchers {\n\t\t\t// be fair to other store operations by yielding time taken\n\t\t\tdelayTicker.Reset(syncDuration)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-delayTicker.C:\n\t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// syncVictimsLoop tries to write precomputed watcher responses to\n// watchers that had a blocked watcher channel\nfunc (s *watchableStore) syncVictimsLoop() {\n\tdefer s.wg.Done()\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tfor s.moveVictims() != 0 {\n\t\t\t// try to update all victim watchers\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n\t\tisEmpty := len(s.victims) == 0\n\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t\tvar tickc <-chan time.Time\n\t\tif !isEmpty {\n\t\t\ttickc = time.After(10 * time.Millisecond)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-tickc:\n\t\tcase <-s.victimc:\n\t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// moveVictims tries to update watches with already pending event data\nfunc (s *watchableStore) moveVictims() (moved int) {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tvictims := s.victims\n\ts.victims = nil\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tvar newVictim watcherBatch\n\tfor _, wb := range victims {\n\t\t// try to send responses again\n\t\tfor w, eb := range wb {\n\t\t\t// watcher has observed the store up to, but not including, w.minRev\n\t\t\trev := w.minRev - 1\n\t\t\tif !w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: rev}) {\n\t\t\t\tif newVictim == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tnewVictim = make(watcherBatch)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tnewVictim[w] = eb\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n\t\t\tmoved++\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// assign completed victim watchers to unsync/sync\n\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n\t\ts.store.revMu.RLock()\n\t\tcurRev := s.store.currentRev\n\t\tfor w, eb := range wb {\n\t\t\tif newVictim != nil && newVictim[w] != nil {\n\t\t\t\t// couldn't send watch response; stays victim\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tw.victim = false\n\t\t\tif eb.moreRev != 0 {\n\t\t\t\tw.minRev = eb.moreRev\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif w.minRev <= curRev {\n\t\t\t\ts.unsynced.add(w)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.store.revMu.RUnlock()\n\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\t}\n\n\tif len(newVictim) > 0 {\n\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n\t\ts.victims = append(s.victims, newVictim)\n\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\t}\n\n\treturn moved\n}\n\n// syncWatchers syncs unsynced watchers by:\n//  1. choose a set of watchers from the unsynced watcher group\n//  2. iterate over the set to get the minimum revision and remove compacted watchers\n//  3. use minimum revision to get all key-value pairs and send those events to watchers\n//  4. remove synced watchers in set from unsynced group and move to synced group\nfunc (s *watchableStore) syncWatchers(evs []mvccpb.Event) (int, []mvccpb.Event) {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif s.unsynced.size() == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0, []mvccpb.Event{}\n\t}\n\n\ts.store.revMu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.store.revMu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// in order to find key-value pairs from unsynced watchers, we need to\n\t// find min revision index, and these revisions can be used to\n\t// query the backend store of key-value pairs\n\tcurRev := s.store.currentRev\n\tcompactionRev := s.store.compactMainRev\n\n\twg, minRev := s.unsynced.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactionRev)\n\tevs = rangeEventsWithReuse(s.store.lg, s.store.b, evs, minRev, curRev+1)\n\n\tvictims := w.ch is full.\n\t\t\t// Next retry of syncWatchers would try to resend the compacted watch response to w.ch\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.minRev = max(curRev+1, w.minRev)\n\n\t\teb, ok := eb.moreRev\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: curRev}) {\n\t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tw.victim = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif w.victim {\n\t\t\tvictims[w] = eb\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tif eb.moreRev != 0 {\n\t\t\t\t// stay unsynced; more to read\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.unsynced.delete(w)\n\t}\n\ts.addVictim(victims)\n\n\tvsz := 0\n\tfor _, v := range s.victims {\n\t\tvsz += provided events.\nfunc rangeEventsWithReuse(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, evs []mvccpb.Event, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n\tif len(evs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n\t}\n\t// append from left\n\tif evs[0].Kv.ModRevision > minRev {\n\t\tevs = append(rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, evs[0].Kv.ModRevision), evs...)\n\t}\n\t// cut from left\n\tprefixIndex := 0\n\tfor prefixIndex < len(evs) && evs[prefixIndex].Kv.ModRevision < minRev {\n\t\tprefixIndex++\n\t}\n\tevs = evs[prefixIndex:]\n\n\tif len(evs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n\t}\n\t// append from right\n\tif evs[len(evs)-1].Kv.ModRevision+1 < maxRev {\n\t\tevs = append(evs, rangeEvents(lg, b, evs[len(evs)-1].Kv.ModRevision+1, maxRev)...)\n\t}\n\t// cut from right\n\tsuffixIndex := len(evs) - 1\n\tfor suffixIndex >= 0 && evs[suffixIndex].Kv.ModRevision >= maxRev {\n\t\tsuffixIndex--\n\t}\n\tevs = evs[:suffixIndex+1]\n\treturn evs\n}\n\n// rangeEvents returns events in range [minRev, maxRev).\nfunc rangeEvents(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n\tif minRev < 0 {\n\t\tlg.Warn(\"Unexpected negative revision range start\", zap.Int64(\"minRev\", minRev))\n\t\tminRev = 0\n\t}\n\tminBytes, maxBytes := NewRevBytes(), NewRevBytes()\n\tminBytes = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: minRev}, minBytes)\n\tmaxBytes = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: maxRev}, maxBytes)\n\n\t// UnsafeRange returns keys and values. And in boltdb, keys are revisions.\n\t// values are actual key-value pairs in backend.\n\ttx := b.ReadTx()\n\ttx.RLock()\n\trevs, vs := tx.UnsafeRange(schema.Key, minBytes, maxBytes, 0)\n\tevs := kvsToEvents(lg, revs, vs)\n\t// Must unlock after kvsToEvents, because vs (come from boltdb memory) is not deep copy.\n\t// We can only unlock after Unmarshal, which will do deep copy.\n\t// Otherwise we will trigger SIGSEGV during boltdb re-mmap.\n\ttx.RUnlock()\n\treturn evs\n}\n\n// kvsToEvents gets all events for the watchers from all key-value pairs\nfunc kvsToEvents(lg *zap.Logger, revs, vals [][]byte) (evs []mvccpb.Event) {\n\tfor i, v := range vals {\n\t\tvar kv mvccpb.KeyValue\n\t\tif err := kv.Unmarshal(v); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlg.Panic(\"failed to unmarshal mvccpb.KeyValue\", watchers that watch on the key of the event.\nfunc (s *watchableStore) notify(rev int64, evs []mvccpb.Event) {\n\tvictim := make(watcherBatch)\n\tfor w, eb := range newWatcherBatch(&s.synced, evs) 316→func (s *store) restore() error {\n   317→\ts.setupMetricsReporter()\n   318→\n   319→\tmin, max := NewRevBytes(), NewRevBytes()\n   320→\tmin = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: 1}, min)\n   321→\tmax =    = 10000 // non-const for testing\n\tdefaultCompactionBatchLimit    = 1000\n\tdefaultCompactionSleepInterval = 10 * time.Millisecond\n)\n\ntype StoreConfig struct {\n\tCompactionBatchLimit    int\n\tCompactionSleepInterval time.Duration\n}\n\ntype store struct {\n\tReadView\n\tWriteView\n\n\tcfg StoreConfig\n\n\t// mu read locks for txns and write locks for non-txn store changes.\n\tmu sync.RWMutex\n\n\tb       backend.Backend\n\tkvindex index\n\n\tle lease.Lessor\n\n\t// revMuLock protects currentRev and compactMainRev.\n\t// Locked at end of write txn and released after write txn compactMainRev is the main revision of the last compaction.\n\tcompactMainRev int64\n\n\tfifoSched schedule.Scheduler\n\n\tstopc chan struct{}\n\n\tlg     *zap.Logger\n\thashes HashStorage\n}\n\n// context.Context, ch chan struct{}) {\n\tif ctx == nil || ctx.Err() != nil {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// fix deadlock in mvcc, for more information, please refer to pr 11817.\n\t\t\t// s.stopc is only updated in restore operation, which is called by apply\n\t\t\t// snapshot call, compaction and apply snapshot requests are serialized by\n\t\t\t// raft, and do not be inconsistent, one possible fix is to add s.revMu.RLock() at the beginning of function, which is costly\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\n\ts.b.ForceCommit()\n\th, err := s.b.Hash(schema.DefaultIgnores)\n\n\thashSec.Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n\treturn h, s.currentRev, err\n}\n\nfunc (s *store) hashByRev(rev int64) (hash KeyValueHash, currentRev int64, err error) {\n\tvar compactRev int64\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\ts.revMu.RLock()\n\tcompactRev, currentRev = s.compactMainRev, s.currentRev\n\ts.revMu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif rev > 0 && rev < error) {\n\ts.revMu.Lock()\n\tif rev <= s.compactMainRev {\n\t\tch := make(chan struct{})\n\t\tf := schedule.NewJob(\"kvstore_updateCompactRev_compactBarrier\", func(ctx context.Context) { checkPrevCompactionCompleted checks whether the previous scheduled compaction is completed.\nfunc (s *store) checkPrevCompactionCompleted() bool {\n\ttx := s.b.ReadTx()\n\ttx.RLock()\n\tdefer finishedCompact && scheduledCompactFound == finishedCompactFound\n}\n\nfunc (s *store) compact(trace *traceutil.Trace, rev, prevCompactRev int64, prevCompactionCompleted bool) <-chan struct{} {\n\tch := make(chan struct{})\n\tj := schedule.NewJob(\"kvstore_compact\", func(ctx context.Context) {\n\t\tif ctx.Err() != nil {\n\t\t\ts.compactBarrier(ctx, ch)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\thash, err := {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tprevCompactionCompleted := s.checkPrevCompactionCompleted()\n\tch, prevCompactRev, err := s.updateCompactRev(rev)\n\ttrace.Step(\"check and update compact revision\")\n\tif err != {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\ts.b.ForceCommit()\n}\n\nfunc (s *store) Restore(b backend.Backend) error {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer RevToBytes(Revision{Main: math.MaxInt64, Sub: math.MaxInt64}, max)\n\n\tkeyToLease := make(map[string]lease.LeaseID)\n\n\t// restore index\n\ttx := s.b.ReadTx()\n\ttx.RLock()\n\n\tfinishedCompact, s.compactMainRev),\n\t\t)\n\t\ts.revMu.Unlock()\n\t}\n\tscheduledCompact, _ := UnsafeReadScheduledCompact(tx)\n\t// index keys concurrently as they're loaded in from tx\n\tkeysGauge.Set(0)\n\trkvc, the total pending keys exceeds the restore\n\t\t// chunk size to keep keys from consuming too much memory.\n\t\trestoreChunk(s.lg, rkvc, keys, vals, keyToLease)\n\t\tif len(keys) < restoreChunkKeys RevToBytes(newMin, min)\n\t}\n\tclose(rkvc)\n\n\t{\n\t\ts.revMu.Lock()\n\t\ts.currentRev = <-revc\n\n\t\t// keys in the range [compacted revision -N, compaction] might all be deleted due to would lead to revision decreasing in bbolt db file. In such\n\t\t// a scenario, we should adjust the current revision using the scheduled\n\t\t// compact revision on bootstrap when etcd gets started again.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// See https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/issues/17780#issuecomment-2061900231\n\t\tif s.currentRev < scheduledCompact {\n\t\t\ts.currentRev = scheduledCompact\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.revMu.Unlock()\n\t}\n\n\tif scheduledCompact <= s.compactMainRev {\n\t\tscheduledCompact = 0\n\t}\n\n\tfor key, lid := range keyToLease {\n\t\tif s.le == nil {\n\t\t\ttx.RUnlock()\n\t\t\tpanic(\"no lessor to attach lease\")\n\t\t}\n\t\terr := s.le.Attach(lid, []lease.LeaseItem{{Key: key}})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.lg.Error(\n\t\t\t\t\"failed to attach a lease\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"lease-id\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%016x\", lid)),\n\t\t\t\tzap.Error(err),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\ttx.RUnlock()\n\n\ts.lg.Info(\"kvstore restored\", zap.Int64(\"current-rev\", s.currentRev))\n\n\tif scheduledCompact != 0 {\n\t\tif _, err := s.compactLockfree(scheduledCompact); revision of the KV at the time of opening the txn.\n\tRev() int64\n\n\t// Range gets the keys in the range at rangeRev.\n\t// The returned rev is the current revision of the KV when the operation is executed.\n\t// If rangeRev <=0, range gets the keys at currentRev.\n\t// If `end` is nil, the request returns the key.\n\t// If `end` is not nil and not empty, it gets the keys in range [key, range_end).\n\t// If `end` is not nil and empty, it gets the keys greater than or equal to key.\n\t// Limit limits the number of keys returned.\n\t// If the required rev is compacted, ErrCompacted will be returned.\n\tRange(ctx context.Context, key, end []byte, ro RangeOptions) (r *RangeResult, err error)\n}\n\n// TxnRead represents a read-only transaction with operations that will not\n// block other read transactions.\ntype TxnRead interface {\n\tReadView\n\t// End marks the transaction is complete and ready to commit.\n\tEnd()\n}\n\ntype WriteView interface {\n\t// DeleteRange deletes the given range from the store.\n\t// A deleteRange increases the rev of the store if any key in the range exists.\n\t// The number of key deleted will be returned.\n\t// The returned rev is the current revision of the KV when the operation is executed.\n\t// It also generates one event for each key delete in the event history.\n\t// if the `end` is nil, deleteRange deletes the key.\n\t// Compaction Schedule: Periodic vs Revision-Based\\n\\nThe compaction scheduling is implemented through two strategies in `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/`:\\n\\n**Periodic Compaction** (`periodic.go`):\\n- The `Periodic` struct implements time-based compaction with a configurable retention period\\n- The `Run()` method starts a goroutine that records revisions at regular intervals (every 1/10th of the period)\\n- Keeps a sliding window of revisions and compacts the oldest one once the retention period elapses\\n- Supports different periods: for periods >1 hour, it compacts every hour; otherwise, it compacts every period interval\\n- Implements Pause/Resume functionality for graceful shutdown\\n\\n**Revision-Based Compaction** (`revision.go`):\\n- The `Revision` struct maintains a fixed number of revisions as history\\n- Compacts every 5 minutes, removing revisions older than the specified retention count from the current revision\\n- Simpler strategy than periodic: keeps only N revisions in history\\n\\nBoth strategies are instantiated via the factory function in `compactor.go` using the `New()` function which supports `ModePeriodic` and `ModeRevision` modes.\\n\\n### 2. Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\nRevision index compaction happens at multiple levels:\\n\\n**Store-Level Compaction** (`kvstore.go`):\\n- `Compact(trace, rev)` is the main entry point that accepts a trace and revision number\\n- `updateCompactRev(rev)` updates and persists the compaction revision in the backend storage\\n- `checkPrevCompactionCompleted()` checks if the previous compaction finished before starting a new one\\n- Uses FIFO scheduler to run compaction as a background job\\n- Stores the compaction state using `SetScheduledCompact` and `UnsafeSetFinishedCompact` in the Meta bucket\\n\\n**Batch-Level Compaction** (`kvstore_compaction.go`):\\n- `scheduleCompaction(compactMainRev, prevCompactRev)` iterates through key-value pairs in batches\\n- Deletes keys that are not in the \\\"keep\\\" map (keys that have revisions older than the compaction point)\\n- Processes in configurable batches (default 1000) with sleep intervals to avoid blocking\\n- Computes a hash of the compacted data for consistency verification\\n- Stores metrics about compaction duration, number of keys compacted, and database size\\n\\n**Key Index Compaction** (`key_index.go`):\\n- `compact(atRev, available)` removes versions of keys with revisions <= atRev except the largest one\\n- Removes generations that become empty during compaction\\n- `keep(atRev, available)` identifies which revisions must be preserved (called by the store)\\n- `doCompact()` walks through generations to find the first revision <= atRev\\n- Maintains an \\\"available\\\" map that tracks which revisions need to be kept\\n\\n**Index Interface** (`index.go`):\\n- The `index` interface provides `Compact(rev)` and `Keep(rev)` methods\\n- `treeIndex` implements this interface using a B-tree of `keyIndex` objects\\n\\n### 3. Notification of Watch Streams Spanning Compacted Revisions\\n\\nWatch streams are notified when they span a compacted revision through the `watcher_group.go` implementation:\\n\\n**Watcher Group Compaction Detection** (`watcher_group.go`):\\n- `choose(maxWatchers, curRev, compactRev)` selects watchers to sync and checks for compacted ones\\n- `chooseAll(curRev, compactRev)` iterates through all watchers and identifies those with `minRev < compactRev`\\n- When a compacted watcher is detected (line 251-259), it sends a `WatchResponse` with `CompactRevision` field set\\n- Marks the watcher as compacted with `w.compacted = true` and removes it from the watcher group\\n- If the watcher channel is full, it retries next time during the next sync cycle\\n\\n**Watch Stream Notification** (`watchable_store.go`):\\n- `syncWatchers()` is called every 100ms by `syncWatchersLoop()` to synchronize unsynced watchers\\n- Calls `watcher_group.choose()` which handles the compaction notification\\n- Unsynced watchers are stored in the `unsynced` watcher group\\n- When a watcher's minRev falls below the compaction revision, it receives a compacted notification\\n\\n**Watch Response Types** (`watcher.go`):\\n- `WatchResponse` struct has a `CompactRevision` field that is set when a watcher is cancelled due to compaction\\n- The client receives this response and knows to reconnect with a newer starting revision\\n\\n### 4. Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nSlow watch detection identifies watchers that cannot keep up with the watch stream:\\n\\n**Victim Watcher Handling** (`watchable_store.go`):\\n- When a watcher's channel is full and `send()` returns false, the watcher is marked as a \\\"victim\\\"\\n- Victims are moved to the `victims` batch (line 390-395, 505)\\n- `moveVictims()` runs in a separate loop (`syncVictimsLoop()`) to periodically retry sending to victims\\n- Victims are processed every 10ms, attempting to drain the backlog of events\\n- Once a victim successfully receives its events, it transitions back to synced or unsynced state\\n\\n**Unsynced Watcher Tracking** (`watchable_store.go`):\\n- When a new watch starts with `startRev <= currentRev`, it's marked as unsynced (line 140)\\n- Unsynced watchers are added to the `unsynced` watcher group (line 149)\\n- The `slowWatcherGauge` metric tracks the count of unsynced watchers (line 148)\\n- The `syncWatchersLoop()` processes up to `maxWatchersPerSync` (512) unsynced watchers every 100ms\\n\\n**Metrics** (`metrics.go`):\\n- `slowWatcherGauge` (Prometheus Gauge) tracks \\\"Total number of unsynced slow watchers\\\"\\n- Updated in `syncWatchers()` (line 411): counts both unsynced watchers and victims\\n- Incremented in `watch()` when a watcher starts as unsynced (line 148)\\n- Decremented when watchers are moved to synced or cancelled (line 164, 191, 324)\\n\\n**Watch State Transitions**:\\n- Synced watchers that fall behind become unsynced\\n- Unsynced watchers with full channels become victims\\n- Victims are retried until successful, then transition back to synced/unsynced\\n- Slow watchers that span compacted revisions receive CompactRevision and are removed\\n\\nThis architecture ensures reliable delivery of watch events even under high load, with backpressure handling through victim batches and periodic retry Compaction Schedule: Periodic vs Revision-Based\\n\\nThe compaction scheduling is implemented through two strategies in `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/`:\\n\\n**Periodic Compaction** (`periodic.go`):\\n- The `Periodic` struct implements time-based compaction with a configurable retention period\\n- The `Run()` method starts a goroutine that records revisions at regular intervals (every 1/10th of the period)\\n- Keeps a sliding window of revisions and compacts the oldest one once the retention period elapses\\n- Supports different periods: for periods >1 hour, it compacts every hour; otherwise, it compacts every period interval\\n- Implements Pause/Resume functionality for graceful shutdown\\n\\n**Revision-Based Compaction** (`revision.go`):\\n- The `Revision` struct maintains a fixed number of revisions as history\\n- Compacts every 5 minutes, removing revisions older than the specified retention count from the current revision\\n- Simpler strategy than periodic: keeps only N revisions in history\\n\\nBoth strategies are instantiated via the factory function in `compactor.go` using the `New()` function which supports `ModePeriodic` and `ModeRevision` modes.\\n\\n### 2. Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\nRevision index compaction happens at multiple levels:\\n\\n**Store-Level Compaction** (`kvstore.go`):\\n- `Compact(trace, rev)` is the main entry point that accepts a trace and revision number\\n- `updateCompactRev(rev)` updates and persists the compaction revision in the backend storage\\n- `checkPrevCompactionCompleted()` checks if the previous compaction finished before starting a new one\\n- Uses FIFO scheduler to run compaction as a background job\\n- Stores the compaction state using `SetScheduledCompact` and `UnsafeSetFinishedCompact` in the Meta bucket\\n\\n**Batch-Level Compaction** (`kvstore_compaction.go`):\\n- `scheduleCompaction(compactMainRev, prevCompactRev)` iterates through key-value pairs in batches\\n- Deletes keys that are not in the \\\"keep\\\" map (keys that have revisions older than the compaction point)\\n- Processes in configurable batches (default 1000) with sleep intervals to avoid blocking\\n- Computes a hash of the compacted data for consistency verification\\n- Stores metrics about compaction duration, number of keys compacted, and database size\\n\\n**Key Index Compaction** (`key_index.go`):\\n- `compact(atRev, available)` removes versions of keys with revisions <= atRev except the largest one\\n- Removes generations that become empty during compaction\\n- `keep(atRev, available)` identifies which revisions must be preserved (called by the store)\\n- `doCompact()` walks through generations to find the first revision <= atRev\\n- Maintains an \\\"available\\\" map that tracks which revisions need to be kept\\n\\n**Index Interface** (`index.go`):\\n- The `index` interface provides `Compact(rev)` and `Keep(rev)` methods\\n- `treeIndex` implements this interface using a B-tree of `keyIndex` objects\\n\\n### 3. Notification of Watch Streams Spanning Compacted Revisions\\n\\nWatch streams are notified when they span a compacted revision through the `watcher_group.go` implementation:\\n\\n**Watcher Group Compaction Detection** (`watcher_group.go`):\\n- `choose(maxWatchers, curRev, compactRev)` selects watchers to sync and checks for compacted ones\\n- `chooseAll(curRev, compactRev)` iterates through all watchers and identifies those with `minRev < compactRev`\\n- When a compacted watcher is detected (line 251-259), it sends a `WatchResponse` with `CompactRevision` field set\\n- Marks the watcher as compacted with `w.compacted = true` and removes it from the watcher group\\n- If the watcher channel is full, it retries next time during the next sync cycle\\n\\n**Watch Stream Notification** (`watchable_store.go`):\\n- `syncWatchers()` is called every 100ms by `syncWatchersLoop()` to synchronize unsynced watchers\\n- Calls `watcher_group.choose()` which handles the compaction notification\\n- Unsynced watchers are stored in the `unsynced` watcher group\\n- When a watcher's minRev falls below the compaction revision, it receives a compacted notification\\n\\n**Watch Response Types** (`watcher.go`):\\n- `WatchResponse` struct has a `CompactRevision` field that is set when a watcher is cancelled due to compaction\\n- The client receives this response and knows to reconnect with a newer starting revision\\n\\n### 4. Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nSlow watch detection identifies watchers that cannot keep up with the watch stream:\\n\\n**Victim Watcher Handling** (`watchable_store.go`):\\n- When a watcher's channel is full and `send()` returns false, the watcher is marked as a \\\"victim\\\"\\n- Victims are moved to the `victims` batch (line 390-395, 505)\\n- `moveVictims()` runs in a separate loop (`syncVictimsLoop()`) to periodically retry sending to victims\\n- Victims are processed every 10ms, attempting to drain the backlog of events\\n- Once a victim successfully receives its events, it transitions back to synced or unsynced state\\n\\n**Unsynced Watcher Tracking** (`watchable_store.go`):\\n- When a new watch starts with `startRev <= currentRev`, it's marked as unsynced (line 140)\\n- Unsynced watchers are added to the `unsynced` watcher group (line 149)\\n- The `slowWatcherGauge` metric tracks the count of unsynced watchers (line 148)\\n- The `syncWatchersLoop()` processes up to `maxWatchersPerSync` (512) unsynced watchers every 100ms\\n\\n**Metrics** (`metrics.go`):\\n- `slowWatcherGauge` (Prometheus Gauge) tracks \\\"Total number of unsynced slow watchers\\\"\\n- Updated in `syncWatchers()` (line 411): counts both unsynced watchers and victims\\n- Incremented in `watch()` when a watcher starts as unsynced (line 148)\\n- Decremented when watchers are moved to synced or cancelled (line 164, 191, 324)\\n\\n**Watch State Transitions**:\\n- Synced watchers that fall behind become unsynced\\n- Unsynced watchers with full channels become victims\\n- Victims are retried until successful, then transition back to synced/unsynced\\n- Slow watchers that span compacted revisions receive CompactRevision and are removed\\n\\nThis architecture ensures reliable delivery of watch events even under high load, with backpressure handling through victim batches and periodic retry mechanisms.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
